 468  468 7 WHICH IS PAID BY SICK ELDERLY BENEFICIARIES BEFORE MEDICARE       
 468  468 8 KICKS IN; REDUCING THE PROPOSED PART B PREMIUM INCREASE IN        
 468  468 9 1987, SO THE PREMIUM WILL ONLY INCREASE THAT YEAR BY THE          
 468  46810 RATE OF GENERAL INFLATION, CORRESPONDING TO SOCIAL SECURITY       
 468  46811 COLA ADJUSTMENTS, INSTEAD OF THE RATE OF MEDICAL COST             
 468  46812 INFLATION; PROVIDING FOR CLOSE MONITORING OF PHYSICIAN            
 468  46813 BEHAVIOR UNDER THE PROPOSED PHYSICIAN FEE FREEZE SO AS TO         
 468  46814 PROTECT MEDICARE BENEFICIARIES FROM UNFAIR COST-SHIFTING          
 468  46815 DURING THE 2-YEAR FREEZE PERIOD.  (MOTION FAILED)

 478  478 3 TO AMEND H.R. 1651 WITH AN AMENDMENT IN THE NATURE OF A           
 478  478 4 SUBSTITUTE. H.R. 1651 REQUIRES THE ADMINISTRATOR OF               
 478  478 5 VETERANS' AFFAIRS, AFTER PUBLIIC NOTICE AND COMMENT AND           
 478  478 6 AFTER CONSIDERING THE RECOMMENDATIONS OF AN ADVISORY              
 478  478 7 COMMITTEE AND ITS SCIENTIFIC COUNCIL AND SUBJECT TO JUDICIAL      
 478  478 8 REVIEW, TO PRESCRIBE REGULATIONS GOVERNING THE ADJUDICATION       
 478  478 9 OF THE ISSUE OF SERVICE CONNECTION BASED ON THE DISEASES OF       
 478  47810 CERTAIN VETERANS WHO, DURING SERVICE IN THE ARMED FORCES,         
 478  47811 WERE EXPOSED TO DIOXIN OR RADIATION; AND REQUIRES THAT THE        
 478  47812 ADMINISTRATOR INCLUDE IN SUCH REGULATIONS DETERMINATIONS AS       
 478  47813 TO WHETHER AND UNDER WHAT CIRCUMSTANCES SERVICE CONNECTION        
 478  47814 SHALL BE GRANTED WITH RESPECT TO CERTAIN SPECIFIED DISEASES.      
 478  47815 THE SIMPSON SUBSTITUTE CREATES A GENERAL PUBLIC INFORMAL          
 478  47816 RULEMAKING PROCEDURE THAT WILL PROVIDE THAT THE                   
 478  47817 ADMINISTRATOR WOULD ESTABLISH GUIDELINES AND, WHERE               
 478  47818 APPROPRIATE, STANDARDS AND CRITERIA FOR THE ADJUDICATION OF       
 478  47819 CLAIMS ASSOCIATED WITH THE EXPOSURE TO HERBICIDES OR              
 478  47820 RADIATION FROM AN ATMOSPHERIC WEAPON.  THIS SUBSTITUTE ALSO       
 478  47821 REQUIRES GUIDELINES TO GOVERN THE EVALUATION OF THE FUNDINGS      
 478  47822 OF SCIENTIFIC AND  MEDICAL STUDIES INSURING THAT NEW AND          
 478  47823 STATISTICAL FINDINGS ARE TAKEN INTO ACCOUNT WHEN CLAIMS ARE       
 478  47824 ADJUDICATED.  THE SUBSTITUTE REQUIRES THE VA ADMINISTRATOR        
 478  47825 TO REVIEW ADVICE OF THE ADVISORY COMMITTEE ON ENVIRONMENTAL       
 478  47826 HAZARDS, AND THE COMMITTEE'S SCIENTIFIC COUNCIL REGRADING         
 478  47827 THE DISEASES COVERED UNDER THE AMENDMENT.  THE SUBSTITUTE         
 478  47828 REQUIRES THE ADMINISTRATOR TO MAKE DETERMINATIONS ON SERVICE      
 478  47829 CONNECTION WITH REGARD TO THE DISEASES SHOWING A STRONG           
 478  47830 ASSOCIATION TO AGENT ORANGE EXPOSURE AND RADIATION EXPOSURE       
 478  47831 AS SHOWN IN THE VA'S PROGRAM GUIDE ON RADIATION CLAIMS.
